<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="English">English</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=sparkly&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: English">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=sparkly&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Etymology">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/sparkle#English" title="sparkle">sparkle</a></i> + <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/-y#English" title="-y">-y</a></i>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=sparkly&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Adjective">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en">sparkly</strong> (<i><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#comparable" title="Appendix:Glossary">comparative</a></i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en comparative-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/sparklier#English" title="sparklier">sparklier</a></b>, <i><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#comparable" title="Appendix:Glossary">superlative</a></i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en superlative-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/sparkliest#English" title="sparkliest">sparkliest</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>giving off <a href="/wiki/spark" title="spark">sparks</a>, or small <a href="/wiki/flash" title="flash">flashes</a> of <a href="/wiki/light" title="light">light</a>; <a href="/wiki/glittery" title="glittery">glittery</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/lively" title="lively">lively</a> and <a href="/wiki/high-spirited" title="high-spirited">high-spirited</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/bubbly" title="bubbly">bubbly</a> or <a href="/wiki/effervescent" title="effervescent">effervescent</a></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=sparkly&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: Derived terms">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/sparklies#English" title="sparklies">sparklies</a></span></li></ul>
